```dafny
ghost function MaxOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a > b then a else b
}

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          // z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = y
          // Both x==m and y==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
```

  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;
  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

  if a > b then a else b
}

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;
  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert x == a';
          assert y == a';
          // z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = y
          assert m == x;
          // Both x==m and y==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert x == b';
          assert z == b';
          // y = MaxOf(a',c') <= b' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = z
          assert m == x;
          // Both x==m and z==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert y == c';
          assert z == c';
          // x = MaxOf(a',b') <= c' = y, so m = max(x,y,z) = y = z
          assert m == y;
          // Both y==m and z==m, counterexample contradicts cnt < 2
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0

  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c()) == a();
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c()) == b();
          assert x == b' && z == b';

          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b();
          assert MaxOf(a', c()) == c();
          assert MaxOf(b', c()) == c();
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }

  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')

          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert x == a';
          assert y == a';

ghost function MaxOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a > b then a else b
}

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;
  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          // z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = y
          // Both x==m and y==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {

        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          // z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = y

ghost function MaxOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a > b then a else b
}

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';

          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

          assert x == a' && y == a';

ghost function MaxOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a > b then a else b
}

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        // Determine the maximum among a', b', c'
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
          // z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = y
          // Both x==m and y==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert m == x;
          assert m == y;
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
          // y = MaxOf(a',c') <= b' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = z
          // Both x==m and z==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert m == x;
          assert m == z;
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
          // x = MaxOf(a',b') <= c' = y, so m = max(x,y,z) = y = z
          // Both y==m and z==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert m == y;
          assert m == z;
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

  if a > b then a else b
}

  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }

          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';

          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';

          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }

  if a < b then a else b
}

ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 &&
         MaxOf(a', b') == x &&
         MaxOf(a', c') == y &&
         MaxOf(b', c') == z
      {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert x == a';
          assert y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert x == b';
          assert z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert y == c';
          assert z == c';
        }
        // In each case, two of x,y,z are equal to the largest value,
        // thus at least two of them equal m, contradicting cnt == 1.
        assert x == m || y == m || z == m;
      }
    }
  }
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

ghost function MaxOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a > b then a else b
}

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;
  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert a' == MaxOf(a', b');
          assert a' == MaxOf(a', c');
          assert x == a' && y == a';
          // Since a' is largest, z <= a', so m = a' = x = y
          assert z <= a';
          assert m == a';
          assert x == m && y == m;
          // Both x==m and y==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert cnt >= 2;
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert b' == MaxOf(a', b');
          assert b' == MaxOf(b', c');
          assert x == b' && z == b';
          // Since b' is largest, y <= b', so m = b' = x = z
          assert y <= b';
          assert m == b';
          assert x == m && z == m;
          // Both x==m and z==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert cnt >= 2;
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' == MaxOf(a', c');
          assert c' == MaxOf(b', c');
          assert y == c' && z == c';
          // Since c' is largest, x <= c', so m = c' = y = z
          assert x <= c';
          assert m == c';
          assert y == m && z == m;
          // Both y==m and z==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert cnt >= 2;
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int

ghost function MaxOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a > b then a else b
}

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        // At least one of a', b', c' is the maximum of the three
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
        // In each case, the maximum value (a', b', or c') equals at least two of x,y,z,
        // contradicting cnt == 1 (which says only one of x,y,z equals m).
        // Therefore the assumption of a valid solution leads to a contradiction.
      }
    }
  }
}

ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;
  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      // If a', b', c' were a counterexample, then they would be all positive
      // and would realize the three pairwise maxima.
      // We prove that this is impossible when cnt < 2.
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        // Compute the largest of a', b', c'.
        var M := MaxOf(a', MaxOf(b', c'));
        // Case analysis on which component equals M.
        if a' == M {
          // a' is the largest.
          // Then MaxOf(a',b') = a' = x and MaxOf(a',c') = a' = y,
          // so x == y == a'.
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
          // Since a' = x = y and a' >= z, we have z <= a'.
          // Therefore max(x,y,z) = a' = x = y.
          // Thus both x and y equal m, contradicting cnt == 1.
          assert x == m;
          assert y == m;
          // So this branch cannot occur.
          assert false;
        } else if b' == M {
          // b' is the largest.
          // Then MaxOf(a',b') = b' = x and MaxOf(b',c') = b' = z,
          // so x == z == b'.
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
          // Since b' = x = z and b' >= y, we have y <= b'.
          // Thus max(x,y,z) = b' = x = z.
          // Hence x and z equal m, contradicting cnt == 1.
          assert x == m;
          assert z == m;
          // So this branch cannot occur.
          assert false;
        } else {
          // c' is the largest.
          // Then MaxOf(a',c') = c' = y and MaxOf(b',c') = c' = z,
          // so y == z == c'.
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
          // Since c' = y = z and c' >= a', we have a' <= c'.
          // Thus max(x,y,z) = c' = y = z.
          // Hence y and z equal m, contradicting cnt == 1.
          assert y == m;
          assert z == m;
          // This branch cannot occur.
          assert false;
        }
      }
    }
  }

  if a > b then a else b
}

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          // z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = max(x,y,z) = x = y
          // Both x==m and y==m, so cnt >= 2, contradiction
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
        }
      }
    }
  }
}

ghost function MaxOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a > b then a else b
}

ghost function MinOf(a: int, b: int): int {
  if a < b then a else b
}

// A valid solution: positive a, b, c whose pairwise maxima are exactly x, y, z
ghost predicate IsValidSolution(x: int, y: int, z: int, a: int, b: int, c: int) {
  a > 0 && b > 0 && c > 0 &&
  MaxOf(a, b) == x && MaxOf(a, c) == y && MaxOf(b, c) == z
}

// Does any valid solution exist?
ghost predicate SolutionExists(x: int, y: int, z: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
{
  exists a ::
    exists b ::
      exists c ::
        IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
}

method ThreePairwiseMaximums(x: int, y: int, z: int) returns (possible: bool, a: int, b: int, c: int)
  requires x > 0 && y > 0 && z > 0
  ensures possible == SolutionExists(x, y, z)
  ensures possible ==> IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a, b, c)
{
  var m := x;
  if y > m { m := y; }
  if z > m { m := z; }

  var cnt := 0;
  if x == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if y == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }
  if z == m { cnt := cnt + 1; }

  if cnt >= 2 {
    possible := true;
    a := if x <= y then x else y;
    b := if x <= z then x else z;
    c := if y <= z then y else z;

  } else {
    possible := false;
    a := 0;
    b := 0;
    c := 0;
    // cnt == 1: exactly one of x,y,z equals m = max(x,y,z)
    // Key insight: the largest of any a',b',c' appears in at least 2 pairwise maxima,
    // so the max of x,y,z must appear at least twice. Contradiction with cnt < 2.
    forall a': int, b': int, c': int
      ensures !IsValidSolution(x, y, z, a', b', c')
    {
      if a' > 0 && b' > 0 && c' > 0 && MaxOf(a', b') == x && MaxOf(a', c') == y && MaxOf(b', c') == z {
        if a' >= b' && a' >= c' {
          // a' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=a'=x, MaxOf(a',c')=a'=y, so x==y
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == a';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == a';
          assert x == a' && y == a';
          // Since a' is largest, z = MaxOf(b',c') <= a' = x, so m = x = y
          assert z <= a';
          assert m == x;
          assert cnt >= 2; // contradiction
        } else if b' >= a' && b' >= c' {
          // b' is largest: MaxOf(a',b')=b'=x, MaxOf(b',c')=b'=z, so x==z
          assert MaxOf(a', b') == b';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == b';
          assert x == b' && z == b';
          assert y <= b';
          assert m == x;
          assert cnt >= 2; // contradiction
        } else {
          // c' is largest: MaxOf(a',c')=c'=y, MaxOf(b',c')=c'=z, so y==z
          assert c' >= a' && c' >= b';
          assert MaxOf(a', c') == c';
          assert MaxOf(b', c') == c';
          assert y == c' && z == c';
          assert x <= c';
          assert m == y;
          assert cnt >= 2; // contradiction
        }
      }
    }
  }
}
